ё«б —∆н” «бж“—«Ѕ «б жд”н ббЌяжг… «бгƒё … «б»«ћн ё«∆ѕ «б”»”н «д «бЏб«ё«  «бяжн н… «б жд”н… Џ—нё… жг ћѕѕ… жгЎбж» Ќ«бн« √д  ЁЏб° г‘н—« ≈бм √д «бяжн  я«д  ѕ«∆г«  ”«дѕ  жд” ж жд”  ”«дѕ «бяжн  Ён яЋн— гд «бё÷«н«° ж«Џ »— √д «бЏб«ё«  «бяжн н… «б жд”н… гд Ћж«»  «б”н«”… «бќ«—ћн… «б жд”н….

Report tracks standard of research in Middle East
Highly cited papers are those that rank in the top 1% in terms of citations per paper in their science subject. In mathematics, Egypt and Saudi Arabia perform better than the world average and Turkey, Iran, and Jordan also score relatively well in mathematics and engineering

http://www.nature.com/nmiddleeast/2011/110309/full/nmiddleeast.2011.29.html (http://www.nature.com/nmiddleeast/2011/110309/full/nmiddleeast.2011.29.html)
